6// Sprite image structure - contains pointer, dimensions, and transparent color
7typedef struct {
8 const uint16_t* data;
9 int width;
10 int height;
11 uint16_t transparent; // Auto-detected transparent color
12} SpriteImage;
13
14// Clean, user-friendly macros (PRIMARY - use these!)
15// No need to specify dimensions or transparent color - all auto-detected!
16#define AddSprite(x, y, sprite, scale) \
17 Sprite_Add(x, y, (sprite).data, (sprite).width, (sprite).height, scale, (sprite).transparent)
18
19#define AddFGSprite(sprite, x, y, scale) \
20 Graphics_ForegroundSprite((sprite).data, x, y, (sprite).width, (sprite).height, scale, (sprite).transparent)
